# Fine Tuning Jobs Operations \{#fine-tuning/jobs\}

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/fine\_tuning/jobs \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_jobs\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Get Fine Tuning Jobs_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Get a list of fine-tuning jobs for your organization and user.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<TabbedSection>

<SectionTitle slot="title">

### Code Samples \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_jobs+code-samples\}

</SectionTitle>

<SectionTab slot="tab" id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_jobs+code-samples+typescript">

TypeScript

</SectionTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_jobs+code-samples+typescript">

<TryItNow
  externalDependencies={{"zod":"^3.25.64","@mistralai/mistralai":"latest"}}
  defaultValue={`import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "<YOUR_BEARER_TOKEN_HERE>",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.fineTuning.jobs.list({});

  // Handle the result
  console.log(result);
}

run();`}
/>

</SectionContent>

<SectionTab slot="tab" id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_jobs+code-samples+python">

Python

</SectionTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_jobs+code-samples+python">

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai import Mistral


with Mistral(
    api_key="<YOUR_BEARER_TOKEN_HERE>",
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.fine_tuning.jobs.list()

    # Handle response
    print(res)
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<Operation>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/fine\_tuning/jobs \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Create Fine Tuning Job_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Create a new fine-tuning job, it will be queued for processing.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<TabbedSection>

<SectionTitle slot="title">

### Code Samples \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job+code-samples\}

</SectionTitle>

<SectionTab slot="tab" id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job+code-samples+typescript">

TypeScript

</SectionTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job+code-samples+typescript">

<TryItNow
  externalDependencies={{"zod":"^3.25.64","@mistralai/mistralai":"latest"}}
  defaultValue={`import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "<YOUR_BEARER_TOKEN_HERE>",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.fineTuning.jobs.create({
    model: "Camaro",
    hyperparameters: {
      learningRate: 0.0001,
    },
  });

  // Handle the result
  console.log(result);
}

run();`}
/>

</SectionContent>

<SectionTab slot="tab" id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job+code-samples+python">

Python

</SectionTab>

<SectionContent slot="content" id="operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_create_fine_tuning_job+code-samples+python">

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai import Mistral


with Mistral(
    api_key="<YOUR_BEARER_TOKEN_HERE>",
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.fine_tuning.jobs.create(model="Camaro", hyperparameters={
        "learning_rate": 0.0001,
    })

    # Handle response
    print(res)
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

</TabbedSection>

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/fine\_tuning/jobs/\{job\_id\} \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_get_fine_tuning_job\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Get Fine Tuning Job_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Get a fine-tuned job details by its UUID.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationParametersSection slot="parameters">

</SectionTitle>

<ExpandableProperty
  slot="entry"
  id="job_id"

```python
from mistralai import Mistral


with Mistral(

) as mistral:
```

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/fine\_tuning/jobs/\{job\_id\}/cancel \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_cancel_fine_tuning_job\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Cancel Fine Tuning Job_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Request the cancellation of a fine tuning job.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "<YOUR_BEARER_TOKEN_HERE>",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.fineTuning.jobs.cancel({
    jobId: "6188a2f6-7513-4e0f-89cc-3f8088523a49",
  });

  // Handle the result
  console.log(result);
}

run();`}

```python
from mistralai import Mistral


with Mistral(

    print(res)
```

<OperationTitleSection slot="title">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/fine\_tuning/jobs/\{job\_id\}/start \{#operation-jobs_api_routes_fine_tuning_start_fine_tuning_job\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Start Fine Tuning Job_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Request the start of a validated fine tuning job.

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<TryItNow
  externalDependencies={{"zod":"^3.25.64","@mistralai/mistralai":"latest"}}
  defaultValue={`import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "<YOUR_BEARER_TOKEN_HERE>",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.fineTuning.jobs.start({
    jobId: "56553e4d-0679-471e-b9ac-59a77d671103",
  });

  // Handle the result
  console.log(result);
}

run();`}

```python
from mistralai import Mistral


with Mistral(

) as mistral:

    res = mistral.fine_tuning.jobs.start(job_id="56553e4d-0679-471e-b9ac-59a77d671103")

    # Handle response
    print(res)
```
